                                              We look forward to welcoming you to our desert, and our sunny getaway on the golf course. It is the perfect place to experience the famous desert ambiance.

                                            <div data-reactid="1099">
                                              Enjoy the warm desert breeze with a cocktail by the pool when you arrive  at our sunny retro 2 bed 3 bath home on Tamarisk Country Club golf course. Dine alfresco as the sun sets over the purple mountains. Tomorrow will be a day to remember.

South facing windows let in the views of our stunning mountains, sunrises, sunsets, date palms, golf course and the pool and spa.

Make yourself at home in two spacious, clean and comfortable entertainment areas, three baths, two roomy bedrooms featuring king size beds in both.  More sleeping space is available in the sofa beds.

Bedroom 1: Kingsized Bed and Bath with shower.
Bedroom 2: Kingsized Bed. Shared Bath with tub/shower
Living room:  Sofa bed and loveseat
TV room:  Sectional will sleep two hearty souls, Bath with shower.
We will provide an airmattress if desired. There is plenty of room in the TV Room.
There are 2 water heaters for plenty of hot water, and two A/C units.

The kitchen is fully outfitted with everything you will need to fix your favorite meals. 

You will find a gas BBQ outside the dining room door.

One 42" Samsung smart tv with Dish

We will heat the spa for you at your request at no additional charge.  The pool can be heated at an additional charge of $150 per day 

There is adequate street parking. 

This house is kid friendly if they can swim.

                                            <div data-reactid="1100">
                                              Located on a quiet, exclusive circle with only one entrance to the neighborhood.  The street makes a perfect lap track.

Tamarisk Country Club is a private club (unfortunately, no access for renters) with a rich history.  It's founding members included Frank Sinatra,  Hollywood A-listers in the 1950’s including Danny Kaye, Jack Benny, George Burns, and four of the five Marx Brothers; Groucho, Harpo, Zeppo, and Gummo to name just a few. Tamarisk has hosted 18 Bob Hope Classics since 1960. 

Although Tamarisk is not open to the public, there are countless public golf courses in the area to choose from. If golf, tennis, restaurants and shopping are not enough, there are magnificent hiking trails close by in the canyons and hills surrounding the valley.

                                            <div data-reactid="1471">
                                              This beautiful modern desert style home is located in a quiet and serene neighborhood in the highly sought Tamarisk area in the City of Rancho Mirage.   Home is centrally located to explore all the wonders of the neighboring cities and outdoor recreation sites in the Coachella Valley.

Features and Amenities: 
- Resort quality private home with pool &amp; spa
- Single story, bright, airy, and clean home with south facing back yard
- Fully furnished and tastefully decorated
- Granite Kitchen with newer stainless steel appliances and fully equipped
- Comfortable living Room with sofa set, coffee &amp; side tables, console, flat-screen TV, fireplace
- Family Room &amp; office space with desk, sofa, chair, coffee &amp; side tables, radio/CD Player.
- Dining Room - glass table dining set seat(URL HIDDEN)Master Suite - queen size bed and a private master bathroom
- Guest Suite - queen size bed and a full bath
- Laundry room - washer and dryer
- Clean linens, towels, and toiletries
- Tile floors throughout entire home
- Covered patio with outdoor dining table and chairs
- Desert landscaped surroundings
- Internet/Wi-Fi, Netflix, online streaming, Pandora, DVD player,
- Garage - parking for one car, storage cabinets
- Pool/Spa (no heater)

The home is centrally located with convenient access to the following attractions in the Coachella Valley:
- Cabazon Shopping Outlet
- Palm Springs and the Palm Springs Aerial Tramway
- Sunnylands at the Annenberg Estate in Rancho Mirage
- Agua Caliente Resort and Casino

- Joshua Tree National Park

- Gourmet dining
- Art festivals and galleries
- World famous golf resorts and spas
- Palm Springs Airport
